                    <!-- Carousel banner script -->
                     <!-- Carousel banner script -->
                    <script>//<![CDATA[
                    (function () {

                        var carouselList = [];

                        function CarouselListItem () {
                            this.image = {
                                desktop: 'desktop',
                                tablet: 'tablet',
                                mobile:'mobile',
                                preview: 'preview'
                            };
                            this.copy = {
                                desktop: 'desktop',
                                device: 'device'
                            };
                            this.anchor = {
                                url: null,
                                target: "_self"
                            };
                            this.itemText = {
                            	Heading: 'Heading',
                            	BylineText: 'Byline Text',
                            	previewImage:null
                            };
                            this.contentBanner = {
                            	contentHeading: null,
                            	headlineText: 'headlineTextCopy',
                            	bodyText: 'bodyTextCopy',
                            	bodySubText: 'bodySubTextCopy'
                            };
                        }


                        function populateCarousel() {

                            var swiperSlide = $('#banner').find('.swiper-slide').eq(0).html();
                            $('#banner').find('.swiper-slide').remove(); // remove duplicate slide
                            var swiperSlideThumb = $('#galleryThumb').find('.swiper-slide').eq(0).html();
                            $('#galleryThumb').find('.swiper-slide').remove(); // remove duplicate slide

                            // create slide
                            for ( var item in carouselList ) {
                                $('#banner .swiper-wrapper').append(
                                    '<div class="swiper-slide">' + swiperSlide + '</div>'
                                );
                                $('#galleryThumb .swiper-wrapper').append(
                                    '<div class="swiper-slide slideImage"></div>'
                                );

                            }

                            for ( var i = 0, list = carouselList.length; i < list; i++ ) {
								//console.log(carouselList);
                                // place all banner image variations, but store url in the 'rel' attribute
                                // link-up images otherwise use "#"
                                $('#banner .swiper-slide').eq( i ).prepend(
                                    '<a href="' + ( carouselList[i].anchor.url ? carouselList[i].anchor.url : '#' ) + '" target="' + carouselList[i].anchor.target + '">' +
                                        '<img src="" data-src="' + carouselList[i].image.desktop + '" class="bannerImg bannerDesktop" />' +
                                        '<img src="" data-src="' + carouselList[i].image.tablet  + '" class="bannerImg bannerTablet" />' +
                                        '<img src="" data-src="' + carouselList[i].image.mobile  + '" class="bannerImg bannerMobile" />' +
                                    '</a>'
                                );
                                if (carouselList[i].itemText.previewImage !== null) {
	                                $('#galleryThumb .swiper-slide').eq( i ).prepend(
	                                	'<img class="previewImage" src="' + ( carouselList[i].image.preview ? carouselList[i].image.preview : '#' ) + '" />' +
	                                    '<div class="overlayBanner">' +
	                                        //'<a href="#" class="imgClick">' +
	                                        '<h3 class="headLine">' + carouselList[i].itemText.Heading + '</h3>' +
	                                        '<p class="byline">' + carouselList[i].itemText.BylineText  + '</p>' +
	                                        //'</a>'+
	                                    '</div>'
	                                ); 
                                
                                } else {
	                                $('#galleryThumb .swiper-slide').eq( i ).prepend(
	                                	//'<img class="previewImage" src="' + ( carouselList[i].image.preview ? carouselList[i].image.preview : '#' ) + '" />' +
	                                    '<div class="overlayBanner">' +
	                                        '<a href="' + ( carouselList[i].anchor.url ? carouselList[i].anchor.url : '#' ) + '" target="' + carouselList[i].anchor.target + '" class="imgClick">' +
	                                        '<h3 class="headLine">' + carouselList[i].itemText.Heading + '</h3>' +
	                                        '<p class="byline">' + carouselList[i].itemText.BylineText  + '</p>' +
	                                        '</a>'+
	                                    '</div>'
	                                ); 
                                }
                                
								if (carouselList[i].contentBanner.contentHeading !== null) {
									 // // place all banner copy variations
                                 $('#banner .swiper-wrapper .swiper-slide').eq( i )
                                     .find('.bannerCopy')
                                         .prepend('<div class="grid-container center-block clearfix">'+
					                        '<div class="col-fixed-left">'+
					                            '<img class="phone absolute invisible" src="/Style%20Library/img/goCoverHomePhone.png" alt="Sanlam Go Cover">'+
					                        '</div>'+
					                        '<div class="col-fluid-right">'+
					                            '<div class="col-xs-12">'+
					                                '<h1>' + carouselList[i].contentBanner.headlineText + '</h1>'+
					                            '</div>'+
					                           '<div class="col-xs-12">'+
					                                carouselList[i].contentBanner.bodyText + 
					                               // '<h3 class="subheadText">'+ carouselList[i].contentBanner.bodySubText + '</h3>'+
					                            '</div>'+
					                        '</div>'+
					                            '<div class="col-xs-12" id="appContainer">'+
					                                '<ul>'+
					                                    '<li>'+
					                                        '<a href="/gocover/Pages/default.aspx" class="btn">Find out more</a>'+
					                                    '</li>'+
					                                    '<li>'+
					                                        '<a href="https://itunes.apple.com/us/app/go-cover/id1162067003?ls=1&mt=8" class="apple" target="_blank"></a>'+
					                                    '</li>'+
					                                    '<li>'+
					                                        '<a href="https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=za.co.sanlam.gocover" class="google" target="_blank"></a>'+
					                                    '</li>'+
					                                '</ul>'+
					                            '</div>'+
					                    '</div>');
								} else {
									$('#banner .swiper-wrapper .swiper-slide').eq( i )
                                     .find('.bannerCopy').empty();
								}
                               

                                // place prev image onto the next slide 
                                /* $('#banner .swiper-slide')
                                    // check to see if on last slide
                                    .eq( i == carouselList.length-1 ? 0 : i+1 ) 
                                        .find( '.prevPreview' ).append(
                                            '<img src="' + carouselList[i].image.preview + '" />'
                                        )
                                        .find( '.blurb' ).append(
                                            carouselList[i].copy.desktop 
                                        ); 
								*/
                                // place next image onto the prev slide 
                                /*
                                $('#banner .swiper-slide')
                                    // check to see if on last slide
                                    .eq( i == 0 ? carouselList.length-1 : i-1 ) 
                                        .find( '.nextPreview' ).append(
                                            '<img src="' + carouselList[i].image.preview + '" />'
                                        )
                                        .find( '.blurb' ).append(
                                            carouselList[i].copy.desktop 
                                        ); */
                            }
                        }


                        function getCarouselData() {

                            var origin = window.location.protocol + 
                                    "//" + window.location.host + 
                                    _spPageContextInfo.siteServerRelativeUrl;

                            var winWidth = $(window).width(),
                                desktop = 1280,
                                tablet = 1150,
                                mobile = 555;

                            $().SPServices({

                                operation: 'GetListItems',
                                async: false,
                                listName: 'I like trains Image Carousel Library',
                                webURL: origin,

                                CAMLViewFields:
                                    '<ViewFields>' +
                                        '<FieldRef Name="LinkFilename" />' +
                                        '<FieldRef Name="Banner_x0020_Text" />' +
                                        '<FieldRef Name="Byline_x0020_Text" />' +
                                        '<FieldRef Name="Heading" />' +
                                        '<FieldRef Name="Preview_x0020_Image" />' +
                                        '<FieldRef Name="SortOrder" />' +
                                        '<FieldRef Name="Title" />' +
                                        '<FieldRef Name="BannerText" />' +
                                        '<FieldRef Name="RoutingEnabled" />' /* active field */ + 
                                        '<FieldRef Name="Destination_x0020_URL" />' + 
                                        '<FieldRef Name="Headline_x0020_banner_x0020_copy" />' + 
										'<FieldRef Name="Banner_x0020_Body_x0020_Copy" />' + 
                                    '</ViewFields>',

                                CAMLQuery:
                                    '<Query>' +
                                        '<Where>' +
                                            '<Eq>' +
                                                '<FieldRef Name="RoutingEnabled" />' +
                                                '<Value Type="Boolean">1</Value>' +
                                            '</Eq>' +
                                        '</Where>' +
                                        '<OrderBy>' +
                                            '<FieldRef Name="SortOrder" Ascending="True" />' +
                                        '</OrderBy>' +
                                    '</Query>',

                                completefunc: function ( xData, Status ) {

                                    var maxItems = $(xData.responseXML).SPFilterNode("rs:data").attr("ItemCount") * 1;

                                    var order = null;
                                    var index = 0;

                                    // loop through each item in the list
                                    // -----------------------------------------------------------
                                    $(xData.responseXML).SPFilterNode('z:row').each(function () {
										//console.log($(this));
                                        var sortOrder = $(this).attr('ows_SortOrder');
                                        var title = $(this).attr('ows_Title');
                                        var name = $(this).attr('ows_LinkFilename');
                                        var bannerText = $(this).attr('ows_BannerText');
                                        var link = $(this).attr('ows_Destination_x0020_URL');
                                        var heading = $(this).attr('ows_Heading');
                                        var byline = $(this).attr('ows_Byline_x0020_Text');
                                        var previewImage = $(this).attr('ows_Preview_x0020_Image');
                                        var headlineCopy = $(this).attr('ows_Headline_x0020_banner_x0020_copy');
                                        var bodyCopy = $(this).attr('ows_Banner_x0020_Body_x0020_Copy');
                                        //alert(previewImage);
										//console.log(byline);	
                                        // this only runs on the first item of the list
                                        if ( order == null ) {
                                            order = sortOrder;
                                            carouselList[index] = new CarouselListItem();
                                        }

                                        // this runs when it moves onto the next group of banner items
                                        if ( order != sortOrder ) {
                                            order = sortOrder;
                                            index++;
                                            carouselList[index] = new CarouselListItem();
                                        }
										                                        // if desktop image
                                        if ( title == 'desktop' ) {
                                            carouselList[index].image.desktop = origin + 'I like trains Image Carousel Library/' + name;
                                            carouselList[index].itemText.Heading = heading;
                                            carouselList[index].itemText.BylineText = byline;
                                        }
                                        // if tablet image
                                        else if ( title == 'tablet' ) {
                                            carouselList[index].image.tablet = origin + 'I like trains Image Carousel Library/' + name;
                                            carouselList[index].copy.device = bannerText;
                                        }
                                        // if mobile image
                                        else if ( title == 'mobile' ) {
                                            carouselList[index].image.mobile = origin + 'I like trains Image Carousel Library/' + name;
                                        }
                                        // if preview image
                                        else if ( title == 'preview' ) {
                                            carouselList[index].image.preview = origin + 'I like trains Image Carousel Library/' + name;
                                            carouselList[index].copy.desktop = bannerText;
                                        }
										if( previewImage == true ) {
										    //console.log(previewImage);
											carouselList[index].image.preview = origin + 'I like trains Image Carousel Library/' + name;
											carouselList[index].itemText.previewImage = previewImage;
											//console.log(carouselList[index].image.preview);
											//$('#galleryThumb .swiper-slide').append('<img class="previewImage" src="'+ carouselList[index].image.preview +'" />');

										}  
										//console.log(headlineCopy);
										if(typeof headlineCopy != 'undefined' && typeof bodyCopy != 'undefined') {
											carouselList[index].contentBanner.contentHeading = headlineCopy;
											carouselList[index].contentBanner.headlineText = headlineCopy;
											carouselList[index].contentBanner.bodyText = bodyCopy;
											//carouselList[index].contentBanner.bodySubText = bodySub;

										}											
                                       // get anchor url
                                        // check to see if it needs to open another tab
                                        if ( link ) carouselList[index].anchor.url = link;
                                        link = String (link); // convert to string
                                        if ( link.indexOf("http://www") > -1 || link.indexOf("http://") > -1 || link.indexOf("https://www") > -1 ) { 
                                            carouselList[index].anchor.target = "_blank";
                                        }
                                        
                                    
                                    });
                                }
                            });

                            populateCarousel();
                        }

                        getCarouselData();
                    })();
                
                    
                    
                    
                    //]]></script>

				        // if desktop

				            $(this).find('.bannerDesktop').attr('src',

				            );
				        }
				        // if tablet
				        else if (winWidth > mobile) {
				            $(this).find('.bannerTablet').attr('src', 
				                $(this).find('.bannerTablet').attr('data-src')
				            );
				        }
				        // if mobile
				        else if (winWidth < mobile) {
				            $(this).find('.bannerMobile').attr('src',
				                $(this).find('.bannerMobile').attr('data-src')
				            );
				        }
				
				    });
				
				    }

					  $.each(getId,function(k,v){
					      if(!$('#'+k+'').hasClass('swiper-slide-active')) {
					           $(v).removeClass('activeSlide');

					              $(v).find('.overlayBanner').addClass('activeState');
					          }, 400);
